msg:When I first arrived at the hotel, I felt that the hotel staff were very enthusiastic. Wan Junlan, the lobby manager, and Xiaoxue at the front desk arranged the check-in enthusiastically and meticulously. When you get to the room, the facilities are advanced, and you can use face recognition to enter and exit the room, so you don't have to worry about forgetting your key card. Service staff Wang Fei and Sun Deshu not only brought welcome fruit plates and desserts, but also carefully introduced the surrounding conditions, and the hygiene work was also meticulous. At breakfast the next day, Xiao He, the service staff of the Chinese food depar**ent in the breakfast room, was busy and helped to serve coffee and desserts. He was warm and thoughtful. The restaurant has a complete range of items, especially the special noodles and large intestine noodles, which are not available in other hotels. They are clean and delicious. When I went out to pick up the car, I found that the car had been carefully washed. Looking at the love card next to the car, it turned out that the security guard Wang Hongfu had already washed it. This stay made us all feel at home, and we will stay at Jinfeng Hotel next time.
